 Political equation of jhalawar-baran seat After Independence, this seat was only Jhalawar but in the delimitation of 2008 jhalawar-baran parliamentary constituency was constituted by combining 4 assembly seats of Jhalawar district and 4 assembly seats of Baran district
 yahaan ab tak hue kul 16 loksabhaa chunaav main sabase zyada bijepi ne 8 baar jeet darj kii
